text-decoration: none;\">                          <h1 style=\"mso-line-height-rule: exactly; font-family: 'Helvetica', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 48px; font-weight: 600; letter-spacing: -.03em; line-height: 52px; margin: 0 0 24px;\">From local governance to global forums, policy drives it all.</h1>   <br>                                                                                       <!-- START p.html -->                                                                     <p class=\"degrees-hero\" align=\"left\" dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-weight: 'normal'; Understanding how policies are made, implemented, and evaluated gives you the power to shape change that truly matters.<br><br>The <b>Master’s in Public Policy (MA-PP)</b> from <b>O.P. Jindal Global University</b> equips you with the insights, tools, and networks to influence decision-making and lead in complex environments.                                                                    </p>                                        <!-- END p.html-->                                                    <!-- START p.html -->                                 <div style=\"height: 24px;\">&nbsp;</div>                                        <p class=\"degrees-hero\" align=\"left\" dir=\"ltr\" style=\"font-weight: 'normal';
